      </table>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">
        British Overseas Territories citizen
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       None of the overseas territories has its own nationality status, and all citizens are classed as
       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">
        British Overseas Territories citizens
       </a>
       (BOTC). They do, however, have legislative independence over immigration, and holding the status of a BOTC does not automatically give a person a right of abode in any of the territories, as it depends on the territory's immigration laws. A territory may issue
       <a href="/wiki/Belonger_status" title="Belonger status">
        Belonger status
       </a>
       to allow a person classed as a BOTC to reside in the territory that they have close links with. Non-BOTC citizens may acquire Belonger status to reside in a particular territory (and may subsequently become naturalised BOTC if they wish).
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_National_Day_011_(9719769048)_(3).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1310" data-file-width="1969" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/220px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/330px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg/440px-Gibraltar_National_Day_011_%289719769048%29_%283%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Gibraltar_National_Day_011_(9719769048)_(3).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Thousands of
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gibraltarian_people" title="Gibraltarian people">
          Gibraltarians
         </a>
         dress in their national colours of red and white during the 2013
         <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar_National_Day" title="Gibraltar National Day">
          Gibraltar National Day
         </a>
         celebrations.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Historically, most inhabitants of the British Empire held the status of
       <a href="/wiki/British_subject" title="British subject">
        British subject
       </a>
       , which was usually lost upon independence. From 1949, British subjects in the United Kingdom and the remaining colonies became
       <a href="/wiki/History_of_British_nationality_law" title="History of British nationality law">
        citizens of the United Kingdom and Colonies
       </a>
       . However changes in British immigration and nationality law between 1962 and 1983 saw the creation of a separate British Dependent Territories citizenship (BDTC) with effect from January 1983. Citizens in most territories were stripped of full British citizenship. This was mainly to prevent a mass exodus of the citizens of Hong Kong to the UK before the agreed handover to China in 1997. Exception was made for the
       <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">
        Falkland Islands
       </a>
       , which had been invaded in 1982 by
       <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
        Argentina
       </a>
       . Full British citizenship was soon returned to the people of
       <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">
        Gibraltar
       </a>
       having regard to the friction with Spain.
      </p>
      <p>
       However, the
       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_Act_2002" title="British Overseas Territories Act 2002">
        British Overseas Territories Act 2002
       </a>
       replaced British Dependent Territory citizenship with
       <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories_citizen" title="British Overseas Territories citizen">
        British Overseas Territories citizenship
       </a>
       (BOTC), and restored full British citizenship to all BOTCs except those from Akrotiri and Dhekelia. This restored to BOTCs the right to reside in the UK.
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/British_nationality_law" title="British nationality law">
        British citizens
       </a>
       , however, do not have an automatic right to reside in any of the Overseas Territories. Some territories prohibit immigration, and any visitors are required to seek the permission of the territory's government to live in the territory.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Military">
        Military
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Military">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2592" data-file-width="3888" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/220px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/330px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg/440px-Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mount_Pleasant_Airport_-_Donald_Morrison.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/RAF_Mount_Pleasant" title="RAF Mount Pleasant">
          RAF Mount Pleasant
         </a>
         , Falkland Islands
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Defence of the Overseas Territories is the responsibility of the UK. Many of the overseas territories are used as military bases by the UK and its allies.
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Ascension_Island" title="Ascension Island">
         Ascension Island
        </a>
        (part of
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena,_Ascension_and_Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha">
         Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha
        </a>
        ) – the Base known as
        <a href="/wiki/RAF_Ascension_Island" title="RAF Ascension Island">
         RAF Ascension Island
        </a>
        is used by both the
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">
         Royal Air Force
        </a>
        and the
        <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">
         United States Air Force
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">
         Bermuda
        </a>
        – became the primary
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">
         Royal Navy
        </a>
        base in America, following US independence. The Naval establishment included an admiralty, a
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Naval_Dockyard,_Bermuda" title="Royal Naval Dockyard, Bermuda">
         dockyard
        </a>
        , and a naval squadron. A considerable
        <a href="/wiki/Bermuda_Garrison" title="Bermuda Garrison">
         military garrison
        </a>
        was built up to protect it, and Bermuda, which the British Government came to see as a base, rather than as a colony, was known as
        <i>
         Fortress Bermuda
        </i>
        , and the
        <i>
         Gibraltar of the West
        </i>
        (Bermudians, like Gibraltarians, also dub their territory "The Rock").
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">
         <a href="#cite_note-57">
          [57]
         </a>
        </sup>
        Canada and the USA also established bases in Bermuda during the Second World War, which were maintained through the
        <a href="/wiki/Cold_War" title="Cold War">
         Cold War
        </a>
        . Four air bases were located in Bermuda during the Second World War (operated by the Royal Air Force, Royal Navy, US Navy, and US Army/Army Air Force). Since 1995, the
        <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Bermuda" title="Military of Bermuda">
         military force in Bermuda
        </a>
        has been reduced to the local
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Territorial_Army_(United_Kingdom)" title="Territorial Army (United Kingdom)">
         territorial
        </a>
        battalion, the
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Bermuda_Regiment" title="Royal Bermuda Regiment">
         Royal Bermuda Regiment
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/British_Indian_Ocean_Territory" title="British Indian Ocean Territory">
         British Indian Ocean Territory
        </a>
        – the island of
        <a href="/wiki/Diego_Garcia" title="Diego Garcia">
         Diego Garcia
        </a>
        is home to a large naval base and airbase leased to the United States by the United Kingdom until 2036 (unless renewed). There are British forces in small numbers in the BIOT for administrative and immigration purposes.
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">
         Falkland Islands
        </a>
        – the
        <a href="/wiki/Military_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="Military of the Falkland Islands">
         British Forces Falkland Islands
        </a>
        includes commitments from the
        <a href="/wiki/British_Army" title="British Army">
         British Army
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">
         Royal Air Force
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">
         Royal Navy
        </a>
        , along with the
        <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands_Defence_Force" title="Falkland Islands Defence Force">
         Falkland Islands Defence Force
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">
         Gibraltar
        </a>
        –
        <a href="/wiki/British_Forces_Gibraltar" title="British Forces Gibraltar">
         British Forces Gibraltar
        </a>
        includes a Royal Navy
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cammell_Laird_Gibraltar" title="Cammell Laird Gibraltar">
         dockyard
        </a>
        (also used by
        <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">
         NATO
        </a>
        ),
        <a href="/wiki/RAF_Gibraltar" title="RAF Gibraltar">
         RAF Gibraltar
        </a>
        – used by the RAF and NATO and a local garrison – the
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Gibraltar_Regiment" title="Royal Gibraltar Regiment">
         Royal Gibraltar Regiment
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        The Sovereign Base Areas of
        <a href="/wiki/Akrotiri_and_Dhekelia" title="Akrotiri and Dhekelia">
         Akrotiri and Dhekelia
        </a>
        in Cyprus – maintained as strategic British military bases in the eastern
        <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">
         Mediterranean Sea
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Montserrat" title="Montserrat">
         Montserrat
        </a>
        – the
        <a href="/wiki/Royal_Montserrat_Defence_Force" title="Royal Montserrat Defence Force">
         Royal Montserrat Defence Force
        </a>
        , historically connected with the Irish Guards, is a body of twenty volunteers, whose duties are primarily ceremonial.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">
         <a href="#cite_note-58">
          [58]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena" title="Saint Helena">
         Saint Helena
        </a>
        – it has been speculated
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">
         <a href="#cite_note-59">
          [59]
         </a>
        </sup>
        that the new
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena_Airport" title="Saint Helena Airport">
         Saint Helena Airport
        </a>
        might be used for military purposes but this has neither been confirmed nor denied.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">
        Languages
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Languages">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1728" data-file-width="2592" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/220px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/330px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg/440px-Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands-113070.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Cliff" title="Cliff">
          Cliffs
         </a>
         at
         <a href="/wiki/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands" title="Gough and Inaccessible Islands">
          Gough and Inaccessible Islands
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Most of the languages other than English spoken in the territories contain a large degree of English, either as a root language, or in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Codeswitching" title="Codeswitching">
        codeswitching
       </a>
       , e.g. Llanito. They include:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Llanito" title="Llanito">
         Llanito
        </a>
        or Yanito and
        <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">
         Spanish
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">
         Gibraltar
        </a>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cayman_Creole" title="Cayman Creole">
         Cayman Creole
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">
         Cayman Islands
        </a>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">
         Portuguese
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">
         Bermuda
        </a>
        )
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">
         <a href="#cite_note-60">
          [60]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks-Caicos_Creole" title="Turks-Caicos Creole">
         Turks-Caicos Creole
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">
         Turks and Caicos Islands
        </a>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pitkern" title="Pitkern">
         Pitkern
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">
         Pitcairn Islands
        </a>
        )
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Forms of English:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Bermudian_English" title="Bermudian English">
         Bermudian English
        </a>
        (
        <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">
         Bermuda
        </a>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands_English" title="Falkland Islands English">
         Falkland Islands English
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Currencies">
        Currencies
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Currencies">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_British_currencies" title="List of British currencies">
        List of British currencies
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The many British overseas territories use a varied assortment of currencies, including the euro, pound, US dollar, NZ dollar, or their own currencies, which may be pegged to one of these.

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Symbols_and_insignia">
        Symbols and insignia
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Symbols and insignia">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Overseas_Territories_flags_(8958664223).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1424" data-file-width="2136" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg/220px-Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg/330px-Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg/440px-Overseas_Territories_flags_%288958664223%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Overseas_Territories_flags_(8958664223).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Overseas Territories flags in Parliament Square in 2013
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Each overseas territory has been granted its own flag and coat of arms by the British monarch. Traditionally, the flags follow the
       <a href="/wiki/Blue_Ensign" title="Blue Ensign">
        Blue Ensign
       </a>
       design, with the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Flag" title="Union Flag">
        Union Flag
       </a>
       in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flag_terminology" title="Flag terminology">
        canton
       </a>
       , and the territory's coat of arms in the fly. Exceptions to this are Bermuda which uses a
       <a href="/wiki/Red_Ensign" title="Red Ensign">
        Red Ensign
       </a>
       ; British Antarctic Territory which uses a
       <a href="/wiki/White_Ensign" title="White Ensign">
        White Ensign
       </a>
       ; British Indian Ocean Territory which uses a Blue Ensign with wavy lines to symbolise the sea; and Gibraltar which uses a banner of its
       <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Gibraltar" title="Coat of arms of Gibraltar">
        coat of arms
       </a>
       (the
       <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Gibraltar" title="Flag of Gibraltar">
        flag of the city of Gibraltar
       </a>
       ).
      </p>
      <p>
       Akrotiri and Dhekelia and
       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena,_Ascension_and_Tristan_da_Cunha" title="Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha">
        Saint Helena, Ascension and Tristan da Cunha
       </a>
       are the only British overseas territories without their own flag. The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Flag" title="Union Flag">
        Union Flag
       </a>
       is used in these territories.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">
        Sports
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Sports">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">
        Bermuda
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/British_Virgin_Islands" title="British Virgin Islands">
        British Virgin Islands
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">
        Cayman Islands
       </a>
       are the only British Overseas Territories with recognised
       <a href="/wiki/National_Olympic_Committee" title="National Olympic Committee">
        National Olympic Committees
       </a>
       (NOCs); the
       <a href="/wiki/British_Olympic_Association" title="British Olympic Association">
        British Olympic Association
       </a>
       is recognised as the appropriate NOC for athletes from the other territories, and thus athletes who hold a British passport are eligible to represent Great Britain at the Olympic Games.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">
        <a href="#cite_note-67">
         [67]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Shara_Proctor" title="Shara Proctor">
        Shara Proctor
       </a>
       from
       <a href="/wiki/Anguilla" title="Anguilla">
        Anguilla
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Delano_Williams" title="Delano Williams">
        Delano Williams
       </a>
       from the
       <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">
        Turks and Caicos Islands
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Jenaya_Wade-Fray" title="Jenaya Wade-Fray">
        Jenaya Wade-Fray
       </a>
       from Bermuda
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">
        <a href="#cite_note-68">
         [68]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Georgina_Cassar" title="Georgina Cassar">
        Georgina Cassar
       </a>
       from
       <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar" title="Gibraltar">
        Gibraltar
       </a>
       strived to represent
       <a href="/wiki/Team_GB" title="Team GB">
        Team GB
       </a>
       at the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/London_2012_Olympics" title="London 2012 Olympics">
        London 2012 Olympics
       </a>
       . Proctor, Wade-Fray and Cassar qualified for Team GB, with Williams missing the cut, however wishing to represent the UK in 2016.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">
        <a href="#cite_note-69">
         [69]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">
        <a href="#cite_note-70">
         [70]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Gibraltar_national_football_team" title="Gibraltar national football team">
        Gibraltar national football team
       </a>
       was accepted into
       <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">
        UEFA
       </a>
       in 2013 in time for the 2016 European Championships. It has also applied to be part of
       <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">
        FIFA
       </a>
       and hopes to be accepted in time for eligibility for the 2018 FIFA World Cup qualifying.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Biodiversity">
        Biodiversity
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Biodiversity">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;">
        <div class="noresize">
         <map name="ImageMap_1_1456130565">
          <area alt="Historic Town of St George and Related Fortifications, Bermuda" coords="224,158,367,217" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site:_Historic_Town_of_St_George_and_Related_Fortifications,_Bermuda" shape="rect" title="Historic Town of St George and Related Fortifications, Bermuda"/>
          <area alt="Gough and Inaccessible Islands" coords="366,349,487,412" href="/wiki/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands" shape="rect" title="Gough and Inaccessible Islands"/>
          <area alt="Henderson Island" coords="35,305,170,341" href="/wiki/Henderson_Island_(Pitcairn_Islands)" shape="rect" title="Henderson Island"/>
          <area alt="Gorham's Cave" coords="267,120,408,156" href="/wiki/Gorham%27s_Cave" shape="rect" title="Gorham's Cave"/>
         </map>
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="552" data-file-width="540" height="511" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg/500px-BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg/750px-BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg/1000px-BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg.png 2x" usemap="#ImageMap_1_1456130565" width="500"/>
        </div>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:BOT_World_Heritage_Sites_Map.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The World Heritage Sites of the UK (Overseas Territories): The natural sites of
         <a href="/wiki/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands" title="Gough and Inaccessible Islands">
          Gough and Inaccessible Islands
         </a>
         and
         <a href="/wiki/Henderson_Island_(Pitcairn_Islands)" title="Henderson Island (Pitcairn Islands)">
          Henderson Island
         </a>
         are marked green, the cultural sites of the
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site:_Historic_Town_of_St_George_and_Related_Fortifications,_Bermuda" title="UNESCO World Heritage Site: Historic Town of St George and Related Fortifications, Bermuda">
          Historic Town of St George and Related Fortifications
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/wiki/Kourion" title="Kourion">
          Kourion
         </a>
         , and
         <a href="/wiki/Gorham%27s_Cave" title="Gorham's Cave">
          Gorham's Cave
         </a>
         are marked red.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The British Overseas Territories have more biodiversity than the entire UK mainland.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ukotcf.org_71-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-ukotcf.org-71">
         [71]
        </a>
       </sup>
       There are at least 180
       <a href="/wiki/Endemism" title="Endemism">
        endemic plant species
       </a>
       in the overseas territories as opposed to only 12 on the UK mainland. Responsibility for protection of biodiversity and meeting obligations under international environmental conventions is shared between the UK Government and the local governments of the territories.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kew.org_72-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-kew.org-72">
         [72]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Two areas,
       <a href="/wiki/Henderson_Island_(Pitcairn_Islands)" title="Henderson Island (Pitcairn Islands)">
        Henderson Island
       </a>
       in the
       <a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">
        Pitcairn Islands
       </a>
       as well as the
       <a href="/wiki/Gough_and_Inaccessible_Islands" title="Gough and Inaccessible Islands">
        Gough and Inaccessible Islands
       </a>
       of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tristan_Da_Cunha" title="Tristan Da Cunha">
        Tristan Da Cunha
       </a>
       are listed as
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site" title="UNESCO World Heritage Site">
        UNESCO World Heritage Sites
       </a>
       , and two other territories, the
       <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">
        Turks and Caicos Islands
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena" title="Saint Helena">
        Saint Helena
       </a>
       are on the United Kingdom's tentative list for future
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNESCO_World_Heritage_Site" title="UNESCO World Heritage Site">
        UNESCO World Heritage Sites
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">
        <a href="#cite_note-73">
         [73]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">
        <a href="#cite_note-74">
         [74]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Gibraltar's
       <a href="/wiki/Gorham%27s_Cave" title="Gorham's Cave">
        Gorham's Cave
       </a>
       Complex is also found on the UK's tentative UNESCO World Heritage Site list.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">
        <a href="#cite_note-75">
         [75]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The three regions of biodiversity hotspots situated in the British Overseas Territories are the
       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">
        Caribbean
       </a>
       Islands, the
       <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Basin" title="Mediterranean Basin">
        Mediterranean Basin
       </a>
       and the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oceania_ecozone" title="Oceania ecozone">
        Oceania ecozone
       </a>
       in the Pacific.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kew.org_72-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-kew.org-72">
         [72]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The UK created the largest continuous
       <a href="/wiki/Marine_protected_area" title="Marine protected area">
        marine protected areas
       </a>
       in the world, the
       <a href="/wiki/Chagos_Marine_Protected_Area" title="Chagos Marine Protected Area">
        Chagos Marine Protected Area
       </a>
       , and announced in 2015 funding to establish a new, larger, reserve around the Pitcairn Islands.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">
        <a href="#cite_note-76">
         [76]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">
        <a href="#cite_note-77">
         [77]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">
        <a href="#cite_note-78">
         [78]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In January 2016, the UK government announced the intention to create a marine protected area around
       <a href="/wiki/Ascension_Island" title="Ascension Island">
        Ascension Island
       </a>
       . The protected area would be 234,291 square kilometers, half of which would be closed to fishing.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">
        <a href="#cite_note-79">
         [79]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">
        References
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=British_Overseas_Territories&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: References">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">
       <ol class="references">
        <li id="cite_note-fco-1">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-fco_1-0">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <cite class="citation web">
           <a class="external text" href="https://www.gov.uk/government/policies/protecting-and-developing-the-overseas-territories" rel="nofollow">
            "Supporting the Overseas Territories"
           </a>
           . UK Government
           <span class="reference-accessdate">
            . Retrieved
            <span class="nowrap">
             8 November
            </span>
            2014
           </span>
           .
           <q>
            There are 14 Overseas Territories which retain a constitutional link with the UK. .... Most of the Territories are largely self-governing, each with its own constitution and its own government, which enacts local laws. Although the relationship is rooted in four centuries of shared history, the UK government's relationship with its Territories today is a modern one, based on mutual benefits and responsibilities. The foundations of this relationship are partnership, shared values and the right of the people of each territory to choose to freely choose whether to remain a British Overseas Territory or to seek an alternative future.
           </q>
          </cite>
          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Supporting+the+Overseas+Territories&amp;rft.pub=UK+Government&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.gov.uk%2Fgovernment%2Fpolicies%2Fprotecting-and-developing-the-overseas-territories&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ABritish+Overseas+Territories">
           <span style="display:none;">
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-2">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <b>
           <a href="#cite_ref-2">
            ^
           </a>
          </b>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          <cite class="citation web">
           <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141006173801/http://www.consoc.org.uk/other-content/about-us/discover-the-facts/what-is-the-british-constitution/in-detail/" rel="nofollow">
            "What is the British Constitution: The Primary Structures of the British State"
           </a>
           . The Constitution Society. Archived from
           <a class="external text" href="http://www.consoc.org.uk/other-content/about-us/discover-the-facts/what-is-the-british-constitution/in-detail/" rel="nofollow">
            the original
           </a>
           on 6 October 2014
           <span class="reference-accessdate">
            . Retrieved
            <span class="nowrap">
             15 November
            </span>
            2014
           </span>
           .
           <q>
            The United Kingdom also manages a number of territories which, while mostly having their own forms of government, have the Queen as their head of state, and rely on the UK for defence and security, foreign affairs and representation at the international level. They do not form part of the UK, but have an ambiguous constitutional relationship with the UK.
           </q>
          </cite>
          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=What+is+the+British+Constitution%3A+The+Primary+Structures+of+the+British+State&amp;rft.pub=The+Constitution+Society&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.consoc.org.uk%2Fother-content%2Fabout-us%2Fdiscover-the-facts%2Fwhat-is-the-british-constitution%2Fin-detail%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ABritish+Overseas+Territories">
           <span style="display:none;">
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </li>

        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
